<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item&nbsp;2.02.&#160; Results of Operations and Financial Condition</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On December 20, 2004,
Peregrine Systems, Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;) issued a press release regarding the
filing of its Annual Report on Form 10-K for the fiscal year ended March 31,
2004, which includes historical financial results for the fiscal year ended
March 31, 2004.&#160; The filing of the
Company&#146;s fiscal 2004 year-end financial results was delayed due to the
Company&#146;s prior financial restatement, voluntary Chapter II bankruptcy
reorganization proceedings and restructuring activities.&#160; A copy of the press release is attached
hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
information in this report (including the exhibit) is furnished pursuant to
Item 2.02 and shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for the purposes of Section 18 of the
Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to the
liabilities of that Section and is not incorporated by reference into any
filing of the Company, whether made before or after the date of this report,
regardless of any general incorporation language in the filing except as shall
be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. The furnishing
of this report is not intended to constitute a determination by the Company
that the information is material or that the dissemination of the information
is required by Regulation FD.</font></p>

<p style="color:#993300;font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE
RELEASE</font></b></p>

<p style="color:#993300;font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 165.3pt;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Peregrine
Systems</font></b><b><sup><font style="font-weight:bold;">&#174;</font></sup>
Files </b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Annual Report on Form 10-K for the Fiscal Year Ended March&nbsp;31,
2004</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 165.3pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SAN
DIEGO, Dec. 20, 2004</font></b> &#151; Peregrine Systems, Inc. (OTC: PRGN), a
leading provider of enterprise asset and service management solutions, today
filed its annual report on Form 10-K, which includes historical financial
results for the fiscal year ended March&nbsp;31, 2004, with the Securities and
Exchange Commission (SEC).</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 165.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This annual report
includes Peregrine&#146;s financial position at March&nbsp;31, 2004 and 2003, and
the results of its operations and cash flows for the three years ended March&nbsp;31,
2004.&#160; The filing of Peregrine&#146;s fiscal
2004 historical year-end financial results was delayed due to Peregrine&#146;s prior
financial restatement, voluntary Chapter 11 bankruptcy reorganization
proceedings and restructuring activities.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 162.45pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As a result of Peregrine&#146;s
emergence from Chapter 11 reorganization in August&nbsp;2003, the company
adopted fresh-start reporting during the fiscal 2004 second quarter ended Sept.
30, 2003 in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles
(GAAP).&#160; Therefore, Peregrine&#146;s financial
results after the July&nbsp;18, 2003 adoption of fresh-start reporting are not
comparable to results reported in prior periods, because of differences in the
basis of accounting and the capital structure of the predecessor company and
the successor company.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 165.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Peregrine adopted fresh-start
reporting and adjusted the carrying value of its assets and liabilities to their
fair value, effective July&nbsp;18, 2003, when the company&#146;s plan of
reorganization was confirmed.&#160; As a
result, the company re-valued its balance sheet in the fiscal 2004 second
quarter.&#160; Results of operations are
reported for the 109-day period ended July&nbsp;18, 2003 for the predecessor
company, the 257-day period ended March&nbsp;31, 2004 for the successor
company, and the 12-month period ended March&nbsp;31, 2004 on a non-GAAP pro
forma combined basis.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 165.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Historical
GAAP Financial Results and Highlights:</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 165.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Total revenue for the successor
company was $46.0 million for the fiscal 2004 fourth quarter and $125.9 million
for the 257-day period ended March&nbsp;31, 2004&#160;&#160; For the predecessor company, total revenue
was $48.7 million for the 109-day period ended July&nbsp;18, 2003.&#160; The $48.7 million included approximately $5.6
million attributed to transactions initiated prior to fiscal 2003, but for
which the revenue recognition criteria were not fully met until the later
period.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">
 <tr>
  <td width="100%" colspan="2" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:100.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">www.peregrine.com</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>For the successor company, total
license revenue was $17.9 million for the fiscal 2004 fourth quarter and $49.1
million for the 257-day period ended March&nbsp;31, 2004.&#160; This license revenue resulted from license transactions
entered into during the applicable period and, as a result of fresh-start
reporting, does not include any revenue from license transactions initiated
prior to fiscal 2003.&#160; Core product
license revenue for the predecessor company for the 109-day period ended July&nbsp;18,
2003 totaled $13.5 million, which includes $7.9 million from new license
transactions initiated in this period and $5.6 million from license
transactions initiated prior to fiscal 2003.&#160;
Core products include the company&#146;s flagship asset and service
management products, AssetCenter<sup>&#174;</sup> and ServiceCenter<sup>&#174;</sup>, and
certain complementary products.&#160; However,
they exclude products divested by the company in its 2003 fiscal year ended March&nbsp;31,
2003.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 48.45pt;text-indent:-19.95pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>For the three-month period ended March&nbsp;31,
2004, the successor company&#146;s net loss was $6.1 million, or $(0.40) per share
on 15 million shares outstanding.&#160; For
the three-month period ended March&nbsp;31, 2003, the predecessor company&#146;s net
loss was $26.6 million, or $(0.14) per diluted share on 195.4 million shares
outstanding.&#160; For the 257-day period
ended March&nbsp;31, 2004, the successor company&#146;s net loss was $17.9 million,
or $(1.19) per share on 15 million shares outstanding.&#160; For the 109-day period ended July&nbsp;18,
2003, the predecessor company&#146;s net income was $374.2 million, or $1.82 per
diluted share on 208.3 million shares outstanding.&#160; For the year ended March&nbsp;31, 2003, the
predecessor company&#146;s net income was $30.9 million, or $0.16 per share, on
195.2 million shares outstanding.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 48.45pt;text-indent:-19.95pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Peregrine&#146;s cash and cash
equivalent balances, excluding restricted cash, were $105.9 million at March&nbsp;31,
2004. &#160;The non-trade debt of the successor
company totaled $69.3 million as of March&nbsp;31, 2004, including secured
factor loans, senior notes and non-interest bearing notes issued to satisfy
pre-petition debt.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 28.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Historical
Non-GAAP Pro Forma Combined Financial Results:</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 31.35pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Revenue totaled
$174.5&nbsp;million for the pro forma combined fiscal year ended March&nbsp;31,
2004, compared to the $230.0&nbsp;million in revenue reported for the predecessor
company for the fiscal year ended March&nbsp;31, 2003. Pro forma revenue for
core products and services for the combined fiscal year ended March&nbsp;31,
2004 was $174.5&nbsp;million, compared with the $216.1&nbsp;million of revenue
for core products and services reported for the predecessor company for the
fiscal year ended March&nbsp;31, 2003.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 30.45pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>License revenue for the pro forma
combined fiscal year ended March&nbsp;31, 2004 totaled $62.7&nbsp;million. For
this period, $57.1&nbsp;million of the pro forma license revenue was attributable
to license transactions entered into during the period and $5.6&nbsp;million
was attributable to license transactions initiated prior to fiscal 2003, but
for which all revenue recognition criteria were met in the period. License
revenue for the predecessor company for the fiscal year ended March&nbsp;31,
2003 totaled $88.6&nbsp;million, including $3.3&nbsp;million of license fees
for non-core product lines that were subsequently divested in fiscal 2003. For
the fiscal year ended March&nbsp;31, 2003, $59.4 million of the core license
revenue was attributable to license transactions entered into during the fiscal
year and $25.8&nbsp;million was attributable to core license transactions
initiated prior to fiscal 2003, but for which revenue was first recognizable in
fiscal 2003.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 48.45pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Peregrine reported non-GAAP pro forma
net income of $1.2 million, or $0.08 per share, for the three-month period
ended March&nbsp;31, 2004, compared with non-GAAP pro forma net loss of $1.2
million, or $(0.08) per share, for the three-month period ended March&nbsp;31,
2003.&#160; The non-GAAP pro forma results
exclude charges for amortization of intangibles, restructuring, impairments and
bankruptcy reorganization.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 48.45pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The company has
reconciled the non-GAAP pro forma net income (loss) to GAAP net income (loss)
in a table accompanying this press release.&#160;
The pro forma net income (loss) is not prepared in accordance with GAAP
and may be different from non-GAAP financial measures used by other
companies.&#160; Non-GAAP financial measures
should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, measures of
financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Peregrine uses non-GAAP
pro forma information in analyzing financial results because Peregrine&#146;s
management believes that it provides meaningful information regarding the
company&#146;s operating performance and facilitates management&#146;s internal
comparisons to the company&#146;s historical and current operating results and to
the operating results of other companies.&#160;
The company believes that non-GAAP pro forma information is useful to
investors because it allows for greater transparency of the company&#146;s operating
performance.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Management
Commentary</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We are pleased that we
have achieved a major milestone with the filing of our financial results for
fiscal year 2004&#148; said John Mutch, Peregrine&#146;s president and CEO.&#160; &#147;During this fiscal year, the company
achieved important objectives to create a foundation for future success and
growth.&#160; We completed a successful
reorganization, focused and sustained our core business in asset and service
management, and continued to innovate our software offerings. We are diligently
working to file our financial reports for fiscal 2005 as quickly as we can so</font> that our shareholders will have an updated
picture of the progress we&#146;ve made in managing and growing our core business.&#148;</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About
Peregrine</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Peregrine Systems, Inc.
develops enterprise software solutions that enable organizations to evolve
their IT service and asset management practices for reduced costs, improved IT
productivity and service, and lower risk. The company&#146;s asset and service
management offerings &#150; ranging from Peregrine Asset Tracking and Peregrine
Service Establishment to Peregrine Asset Optimization and Peregrine Service
Optimization &#151; address specific business problems. These solutions make it
possible for IT organizations to maintain a changing IT infrastructure, manage
their relationships with end-users and service providers, and gain greater
visibility into how their IT investments are performing. The Peregrine
Evolution Model provides a roadmap for companies that want to systematically
evolve the sophistication and effectiveness of their IT operating practices.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 28.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Founded in 1981,
Peregrine Systems has sustained a rich tradition of delivering solutions with
superior functionality to a broad segment of the global enterprise customer
market. Headquartered in San Diego, Calif., the company conducts business from
offices in the Americas, Europe and Asia Pacific.&#160; For more information, please visit:
www.peregrine.com.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 28.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"># # #</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Peregrine Systems, AssetCenter and ServiceCenter are registered
trademarks of Peregrine Systems, Inc. or its affiliates. All other marks are
the property of their respective owners.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 28.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Risk
Factors</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The financial results described
in this press release are historical, in part because the company has
significant deficiencies, including material weaknesses, in its internal
controls over financial reporting.&#160; Until
the company&#146;s periodic reports are current, investors will not have current
financial information.&#160; For this reason
and based on the other risk factors described in the company&#146;s Form 10-K for
the fiscal year ended March&nbsp;31, 2004, the company believes trading in its
securities at this time is highly speculative and involves a high degree of
risk.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Forward-Looking
Statements</font></b></p>

of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995, particularly

company.&#160; These statements relate to
expectations about future events or results and are based upon information

These forward-looking statements are not guarantees of the future

update or revise any of the forward-looking statements contained herein to
reflect future events or developments.</font></p>

quarterly share amounts may not equal the totals for the respective years.</p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">PEREGRINE SYSTEMS, INC.</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Pro Forma Net Income
(Loss) with GAAP Net Income (Loss)</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(in thousands, except per share amounts;
unaudited)</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)&#160; </font>Successor and predecessor pro forma combined for the 12-month period
ended March&nbsp;31, 2004 represents the addition of the successor company and
predecessor company for the periods noted.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)&#160; </font>Tax benefits have not been recorded in the historical periods in which
the company reported a net loss before income taxes; therefore, pro forma
reconciling items are not presented net of the effects of income taxes.&#160; In the historical periods during which the
company reported net income before income taxes, pro forma reconciling items
have also been presented without a tax effect in order to promote comparability
of the pro forma information for all periods presented.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3) <sup>&#160;</sup></font>Fully diluted shares converted based upon recapitalization of the
company with 15,000 shares on Aug. 7, 2003 retroactively applied to the pro
forma combined 12-month period ended March&nbsp;31, 2004, the three-month
period ended March&nbsp;31, 2003 and the 12-month period ended March&nbsp;31,
2003.</p>
